Volume 49 Issue 1: Public Sector and Non-Profit Co... &gt; A Market Shaping Approach for the Biopharmaceutical... English Français Journal of Law, Medicine &amp; Ethics Article contents Abstract References A Market Shaping Approach for the Biopharmaceutical Industry: Governing Innovation Towards the Public Interest Published online by Cambridge University Press: 21 April 2021 Mariana Mazzucato &nbsp;and Henry Lishi Li Article Metrics Article contents Abstract References Get access Share Cite Rights &amp; Permissions [Opens in a new window] Abstract Enhancing research and development and ensuring equitable pricing and access to cutting-edge treatments are both vital to a biopharmaceutical innovation system that works in the public interest. However, despite delivering numerous therapeutic advances, the existing system suffers from major problems: a lack of directionality to meet key needs, inefficient collaboration, high prices that fail to reflect the public contribution, and an overly-financialized business model. Keywords Pharmaceutical Innovation Pricing Access Governance Information Type Symposium Articles Information Journal of Law, Medicine &amp; Ethics , Volume 49 , Issue 1: Public Sector and Non-Profit Contributions to Drug Development: Historical Scope, Opportunities, and Challenges , Spring 2021 , pp. 39 - 49 DOI: https://doi.org/10.1017/jme.2021.8 [Opens in a new window] Copyright © 2021 The Author(s) Access options Get access to the full version of this content by using one of the access options below.
